### [1] [Exploiting Repetitions and Interference Cancellation for the 6G-V2X Sidelink Autonomous Mode](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03039)
*Alessandro Bazzi,Vittorio Todisco,Antonella Molinaro,Antoine O. Berthet,Richard A. Stirling-Gallacher,Claudia Campolo*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 该论文提出利用具备连续干扰消除（SIC）能力的接收机，通过解码并抵消重复传输的包来缓解NR-V2X Mode 2中的干扰和冲突问题，从而显著提升高干扰场景下的通信可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 3GPP开发的NR-V2X标准中，Mode 2信道接入方案允许车辆自主选择无线资源，但在动态移动环境中易受干扰和包碰撞影响，导致性能下降。虽然通过发送多个包副本可提高可靠性，但这会增加信道拥塞，亟需一种能高效利用重复传输而不加剧拥塞的新机制。

Method: 提出利用配备连续干扰消除（SIC）功能的接收机，在成功解码一个包后，将其干扰分量从未来或过去的接收信号中消除，从而能够解码后续或之前的新包，有效利用重复传输而无需额外增加信道负载。

Result: 在高速公路场景的大量仿真表明，所提方案显著优于传统Mode 2方案，特别是在高干扰条件下，部分场景下的性能提升超过100%。

Conclusion: 通过结合SIC技术与包重复传输策略，可以突破现有NR-V2X Mode 2的性能瓶颈，在保持可靠性的同时避免信道拥塞恶化，为CAV直接通信提供高效的解决方案。

Abstract: In recent years, the Third Generation Partnership Project (3GPP) has developed the new radio-vehicle-to-everything (NR-V2X) sidelink standard, to enable direct communication between connected and autonomous vehicles (CAVs). Users can autonomously select radio resources for their transmissions with the Mode 2 channel access scheme, which can also operate under out-of-coverage conditions. However, Mode 2 performance is hindered by interference and packet collisions arising from dynamic mobile environments and limitations in assessing radio resource availability. The 3GPP specifications allow transmitting multiple copies of the same packet to improve reliability, though at the cost of increased channel congestion. This paper proposes to leverage receivers equipped with successive interference cancellation (SIC) capabilities, to exploit packet repetitions. Specifically, once a packet is successfully decoded the interfering contribution carried by repetitions can be cancelled from future or past received signals, enabling the decoding of new packets. Extensive highway scenario simulations demonstrate that the proposed solution significantly outperforms the legacy Mode 2 scheme, especially under high interference conditions, achieving improvements exceeding 100% in some cases.

</details>

### [2] [Learning Therapist Policy from Therapist-Exoskeleton-Patient Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02458)
*Grayson Snyder,Lorenzo Vianello,Levi Hargrove,Matthew L. Elwin,Jose Pons*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出患者-治疗师力场（PTFF）和合成治疗师（ST）模型，通过VAE+GMM可视化人机交互动力学，并用LSTM预测治疗师扭矩辅助中风康复机器人。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统中风步态康复依赖治疗师体力参与，过程疲惫且难以维持高强度、长时程与一致性；需降低治疗师负担同时保持干预质量。

Method: 将患者与治疗师的步态运动学编码到共享低维潜在流形（VAE），用高斯混合模型（GMM）学习从患者潜在状态到治疗师响应的概率向量场（PTFF）；另用LSTM在患者-治疗师交互数据上训练以预测治疗师施加的关节扭矩（ST），并集成到ROS外骨骼控制器进行实时扭矩辅助。

Result: 采用留一法交叉验证在8名中风患者上训练与验证；离线结果与初步测试显示，PTFF可解释治疗师行为，ST能生成基于预测治疗师响应的实时扭矩辅助，具备替代/补充外骨骼治疗的潜力。

Conclusion: PTFF提升对治疗师动作的理解以指导策略与控制器设计，ST使治疗师脱离外骨骼持续监测患者细微状态，为中风机器人介导的物理交互康复提供可行新路径。

Abstract: Post-stroke rehabilitation is often necessary for patients to regain proper walking gait. However, the typical therapy process can be exhausting and physically demanding for therapists, potentially reducing therapy intensity, duration, and consistency over time. We propose a Patient-Therapist Force Field (PTFF) to visualize therapist responses to patient kinematics and a Synthetic Therapist (ST) machine learning model to support the therapist in dyadic robot-mediated physical interaction therapy. The first encodes patient and therapist stride kinematics into a shared low-dimensional latent manifold using a Variational Autoencoder (VAE) and models their interaction through a Gaussian Mixture Model (GMM), which learns a probabilistic vector field mapping patient latent states to therapist responses. This representation visualizes patient-therapist interaction dynamics to inform therapy strategies and robot controller design. The latter is implemented as a Long Short-Term Memory (LSTM) network trained on patient-therapist interaction data to predict therapist-applied joint torques from patient kinematics. Trained and validated using leave-one-out cross-validation across eight post-stroke patients, the model was integrated into a ROS-based exoskeleton controller to generate real-time torque assistance based on predicted therapist responses. Offline results and preliminary testing indicate the potential of their use as an alternative approach to post-stroke exoskeleton therapy. The PTFF provides understanding of the therapist's actions while the ST frees the human therapist from the exoskeleton, allowing them to continuously monitor the patient's nuanced condition.

</details>


### [3] [A Novel Modular Cable-Driven Soft Robotic Arm with Multi-Segment Reconfigurability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02468)
*Moeen Ul Islam,Cheng Ouyang,Xinda Qi,Azlan Zahid,Xiaobo Tan,Dong Chen*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出一种模块化、可重构的缆索驱动软体机械臂，通过堆叠多段结构实现可扩展的工作空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决现有软体机器人结构单一、工作空间受限及难以适应多样化应用场景的问题，需要一种具备独立分段控制能力且可灵活扩展的架构。

Method: 采用软硅胶材料制造，设计嵌入式肌腱路由通道及保护性双螺旋肌腱结构；构建可堆叠的多段系统，实现各段的独立控制与模块化组装。

Result: 三段式配置相比单段机械臂，平面工作空间面积增加13倍，体积增加38.9倍；实验证实了硅胶刚度与柔顺性的权衡关系：较软材料提升弯曲灵活性，较硬材料增强结构刚性和承重稳定性。

Conclusion: 通过调节材料刚度可有效平衡柔顺性与强度，该模块化堆叠架构为构建可扩展、可重构的软体机械臂提供了重要潜力和解决方案。

Abstract: This paper presents a novel, modular, cable-driven soft robotic arm featuring multi-segment reconfigurability. The proposed architecture enables a stackable system with independent segment control, allowing scalable adaptation to diverse structural and application requirements. The system is fabricated from soft silicone material and incorporates embedded tendon-routing channels with a protective dual-helical tendon structure. Experimental results showed that modular stacking substantially expanded the reachable workspace: relative to the single-segment arm, the three-segment configuration achieved up to a 13-fold increase in planar workspace area and a 38.9-fold increase in workspace volume. Furthermore, this study investigated the effect of silicone stiffness on actuator performance. The results revealed a clear trade-off between compliance and stiffness: softer silicone improved bending flexibility, while stiffer silicone improved structural rigidity and load-bearing stability. These results highlight the potential of stiffness tuning to balance compliance and strength for configuring scalable, reconfigurable soft robotic arms.

</details>


### [4] [COLREGs Compliant Collision Avoidance and Grounding Prevention for Autonomous Marine Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02484)
*Mayur S. Patil,Nataraj Sudharsan,Veneela Ammula,Jude Tomdio,Jin Wang,Michael Kei,Sivakumar Rathinam,Prabhakar R. Pagilla*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出一种基于凸优化的统一运动规划方法，使海事自主水面船舶(MASS)在实时避碰、遵守COLREGs规则及防搁浅方面实现高效合规航行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MASS虽能解决船员短缺与提升安全效率，但在拥挤水域部署仍面临挑战，亟需具备动态适应性且符合法规的运动规划策略以保障航行安全。

Method: 构建融合速度障碍(VO)避碰约束、COLREGs方向约束及水深防搁浅约束的凸优化框架；扩展VO方法以处理目标船位速估计的不确定性；利用整数线性规划(ILP)将非凸不可航浅水区近似为凸几何体，从而将防搁浅约束纳入优化求解。

Result: 仿真多船会遇场景表明，该方法能生成满足避碰、法规遵从、运动学动力学限制及防搁浅要求的最优可行速度输入，验证了其在实时自主导航中的有效性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 该集成凸优化方法为MASS在复杂动态海洋环境下的实时安全合规航行提供了可行的技术路径，显著提升了系统在拥挤水域的自主决策能力。

Abstract: Maritime Autonomous Surface Ships (MASS) are increasingly regarded as a promising solution to address crew shortages, improve navigational safety, and improve operational efficiency in the maritime industry. Nevertheless, the reliable deployment of MASS in real-world environments remains a significant challenge, particularly in congested waters where the majority of maritime accidents occur. This emphasizes the need for safe and regulation-aware motion planning strategies for MASS that are capable of operating under dynamic maritime conditions. This paper presents a unified motion planning method for MASS that achieves real time collision avoidance, compliance with International Regulations for Preventing Collisions at Sea (COLREGs), and grounding prevention. The proposed work introduces a convex optimization method that integrates velocity obstacle-based (VO) collision constraints, COLREGs-based directional constraints, and bathymetry-based grounding constraints to generate computationally efficient, rule-compliant optimal velocity selection. To enhance robustness, the classical VO method is extended to consider uncertainty in the position and velocity estimates of the target vessel. Unnavigable shallow water regions obtained from bathymetric data, which are inherently nonconvex, are approximated via convex geometries using a integer linear programming (ILP), allowing grounding constraints to be incorporated into the motion planning. The resulting optimization generates optimal and dynamically feasible input velocities that meet collision avoidance, regulatory compliance, kinodynamic limits, and grounding prevention requirements. Simulation results involving multi-vessel encounters demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed method in producing safe and regulation-compliant maneuvers, highlighting the suitability of the proposed approach for real time autonomous maritime navigation.

</details>


### [5] [Generative adversarial imitation learning for robot swarms: Learning from human demonstrations and trained policies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02783)
*Mattes Kraus,Jonas Kuckling*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出基于生成对抗模仿学习的框架，使机器人集群能从人类或策略演示中学习集体行为，并在真实机器人上验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器人集群模仿学习多依赖已有策略生成的演示，缺乏直接从人类演示中学习集体行为的能力。

Method: 采用生成对抗模仿学习（Generative Adversarial Imitation Learning, GAIL）框架，在六项任务中从手动演示和PPO训练的策略演示中学习。

Result: 学习到的行为具有定性意义，性能与原始演示相当；在TurtleBot 4真实机器人集群上的实验显示，行为特征得以保留且性能与仿真一致。

Conclusion: 该框架成功实现了从人类和策略演示中学习可泛化的集体行为，并具备在真实机器人系统中部署的可行性。

Abstract: In imitation learning, robots are supposed to learn from demonstrations of the desired behavior. Most of the work in imitation learning for swarm robotics provides the demonstrations as rollouts of an existing policy. In this work, we provide a framework based on generative adversarial imitation learning that aims to learn collective behaviors from human demonstrations. Our framework is evaluated across six different missions, learning both from manual demonstrations and demonstrations derived from a PPO-trained policy. Results show that the imitation learning process is able to learn qualitatively meaningful behaviors that perform similarly well as the provided demonstrations. Additionally, we deploy the learned policies on a swarm of TurtleBot 4 robots in real-robot experiments. The exhibited behaviors preserved their visually recognizable character and their performance is comparable to the one achieved in simulation.

</details>


### [6] [A Robust Simulation Framework for Verification and Validation of Autonomous Maritime Navigation in Adverse Weather and Constrained Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02487)
*Mayur S. Patil,Nataraj Sudharsan,Anthony S. Saaiby,JiaChang Xing,Keliang Pan,Veneela Ammula,Jude Tomdio,Jin Wang,Michael Kei,Heonyong Kang,Sivakumar Rathinam,Prabhakar R. Pagilla*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种增强的虚拟仿真框架，用于验证和测试海上自主水面船舶（MASS）在复杂海洋环境（特别是恶劣天气和水深地形）下的导航性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 海上自主水面船舶（MASS）的可靠部署需要严格的验证与确认（V&V），特别是在极端和安全关键场景下，而现实世界中的实地测试往往成本高、风险大且难以复现所有条件。

Method: 构建了一个高保真环境建模套件，参数化模拟降雨、雾和波浪动力学等不利天气对海况、感知系统及定位速度的影响；同时集成美国主要港口的高分辨率测深数据，以支持深度感知导航、防搁浅能力及狭窄水域的可控性评估。

Result: 该框架提供了广泛的配置能力，能够系统地在各种海事条件下进行测试，包括那些在实际试验中不切实际或危险的场景，从而有效支持MASS的验证与确认。

Conclusion: 通过结合高保真的气象模拟和精确的水深数据，该虚拟仿真框架为MASS在真实海洋环境中的安全部署提供了强有力的工具，显著提升了验证过程的全面性和安全性。

Abstract: Maritime Autonomous Surface Ships (MASS) have emerged as a promising solution to enhance navigational safety, operational efficiency, and long-term cost effectiveness. However, their reliable deployment requires rigorous verification and validation (V\&V) under various environmental conditions, including extreme and safety-critical scenarios. This paper presents an enhanced virtual simulation framework to support the V\&V of MASS in realistic maritime environments, with particular emphasis on the influence of weather and bathymetry on autonomous navigation performance. The framework incorporates a high-fidelity environmental modeling suite capable of simulating adverse weather conditions such as rain, fog, and wave dynamics. The key factors that affect weather, such as rain and visibility, are parameterized to affect sea-state characteristics, perception, and sensing systems, resulting in position and velocity uncertainty, reduced visibility, and degraded situational awareness. Furthermore, high-resolution bathymetric data from major U.S. ports are integrated to enable depth-aware navigation, grounding prevention capabilities, and evaluation of vessel controllability in shallow or confined waterways. The proposed framework offers extensive configurability, enabling systematic testing in a wide spectrum of maritime conditions, including scenarios that are impractical or unsafe to replicate in real-world trials, thus supporting the V\&V of MASS.

</details>


### [7] [Instant and Reversible Adhesive-free Bonding Between Silicones and Glossy Papers for Soft Robotics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02500)
*Takumi Shibuya,Kazuya Murakami,Akitsu Shigetou,Jun Shintake*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出一种无粘合剂、可溶剂可逆的硅胶-光面纸粘合（SGB）技术，通过简单接触实现牢固界面，支持快速拆卸与重复组装，用于软体驱动器制造。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有流体驱动软执行器的硅胶与非延展材料集成方法依赖不可逆粘合剂或嵌入工艺，存在劳动密集、难以修改和无法复用等问题，亟需一种高效、可重构的替代方案。

Method: 开发硅胶与光面纸的直接接触粘合（SGB），利用表面官能团相互作用及氢键与低聚物扩散的协同效应形成强界面；通过乙醇浸泡实现可逆解粘，无需额外粘合剂或溶剂残留。

Result: SGB界面剪切强度超过61 kPa，可多次拆卸重组而不损失性能；表征表明粘附性主要由纸张表面官能团和硅胶模量决定；基于SGB制造的软执行器在收缩、弯曲和扭转等可编程模式上表现优于或等同于传统嵌入式设计。

Conclusion: SGB提供了一种可扩展、可持续的快速原型制造平台，简化了软体机器人 fabrication 流程，同时支持组件复用与设计迭代，显著提升了软体执行器的工程灵活性与环境适应性。

Abstract: Integrating silicone with non-extensible materials is a common strategy used in the fabrication of fluidically-driven soft actuators, yet conventional approaches often rely on irreversible adhesives or embedding processes that are labor-intensive and difficult to modify. This work presents silicone-glossy paper bonding (SGB), a rapid, adhesive-free, and solvent-reversible bonding approach that forms robust silicone-paper interfaces simply through contact. The SGB interface withstands high mechanical loads (shear strength > 61 kPa) and can be fully detached and reassembled via ethanol immersion without loss of performance, enabling component reuse and rapid redesign. Characterization studies indicate that surface functional groups primarily govern adhesion on the glossy paper and the modulus of the silicone, while durability and environmental response clarify the conditions for reversible debonding. The results further suggest a synergistic interaction of hydrogen bonding and oligomer diffusion, yielding strong yet reconfigurable adhesion. Soft actuators fabricated using SGB design exhibit equal or greater performance compared to conventional embedded-layer design and enable programmable actuation modes, including contraction, bending, and twisting. By simplifying fabrication while supporting reuse and rapid iteration, SGB offers a scalable and sustainable platform for rapid prototyping in soft robotics.

</details>


### [8] [Learning Object-Centric Spatial Reasoning for Sequential Manipulation in Cluttered Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02511)
*Chrisantus Eze,Ryan C Julian,Christopher Crick*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: Unveiler 是一个用于杂乱环境中机器人抓取的新框架，通过将高层空间推理与底层动作执行解耦，显著提升了在密集遮挡场景下的数据效率和成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大规模端到端模型虽然能力强，但在处理密集杂乱环境中的物体检索时，存在数据效率低和缺乏模块化（无法灵活分离感知与决策）的问题。

Method: 提出 Unveiler 框架，核心包含两个模块：1) 基于轻量级 Transformer 的空间关系编码器 (SRE)，通过模仿学习初始化和 PPO 微调，按顺序识别需移除的关键障碍物；2) 旋转不变的动作解码器 (Action Decoder)，负责执行具体抓取动作。该架构实现了高层推理与底层执行的显式分离。

Result: 在仿真测试中，该方法在部分遮挡场景下成功率高达 97.6%，完全遮挡场景下达 90.0%。相比传统端到端策略和大型模型基线，Unveiler 在参数量、推理时间和任务成功率上均表现更优。此外，SRE 的空间推理能力可零样本迁移至真实场景，无需重新训练任何学习组件。

Conclusion: 针对复杂操作任务，采用专门的、以对象为中心的解耦推理架构比单一的大型端到端模型更具优势，能实现更高的计算效率、数据利用率和泛化能力。

Abstract: Robotic manipulation in cluttered environments presents a critical challenge for automation. Recent large-scale, end-to-end models demonstrate impressive capabilities but often lack the data efficiency and modularity required for retrieving objects in dense clutter. In this work, we argue for a paradigm of specialized, decoupled systems and present Unveiler, a framework that explicitly separates high-level spatial reasoning from low-level action execution. Unveiler's core is a lightweight, transformer-based Spatial Relationship Encoder (SRE) that sequentially identifies the most critical obstacle for removal. This discrete decision is then passed to a rotation-invariant Action Decoder for execution. We demonstrate that this decoupled architecture is not only more computationally efficient in terms of parameter count and inference time, but also significantly outperforms both classic end-to-end policies and modern, large-model-based baselines in retrieving targets from dense clutter. The SRE is trained in two stages: imitation learning from heuristic demonstrations provides sample-efficient initialization, after which PPO fine-tuning enables the policy to discover removal strategies that surpass the heuristic in dense clutter. Our results, achieving up to 97.6\% success in partially occluded and 90.0\% in fully occluded scenarios in simulation, make a case for the power of specialized, object-centric reasoning in complex manipulation tasks. Additionally, we demonstrate that the SRE's spatial reasoning transfers zero-shot to real scenes, and validate the full system on a physical robot requiring only geometric workspace calibration; no learned components are retrained.

</details>


### [9] [cuNRTO: GPU-Accelerated Nonlinear Robust Trajectory Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02642)
*Jiawei Wang,Arshiya Taj Abdul,Evangelos A. Theodorou*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: cuNRTO是一个基于CUDA的鲁棒轨迹优化框架，通过两种动态优化架构（NRTO-DR和NRTO-FullADMM）及自定义内核，显著加速了二阶锥规划（SOCP）约束的计算，在仿真中实现了最高139.6倍的速度提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的鲁棒轨迹优化方法虽然能确保自主系统在不确定环境下安全运行，但通常涉及计算成本高昂的大型二阶锥规划（SOCP）约束，限制了其在实时决策中的应用。

Method: 提出cuNRTO框架，包含两种架构：NRTO-DR利用Douglas-Rachford分裂法并行处理SOCP内层子问题；NRTO-FullADMM是一种新型变体，利用交替方向乘子法（ADMM）进一步优化可扩展性。同时使用自定义CUDA核函数进行SOC投影，并利用cuBLAS GEMM链更新反馈增益。

Result: 通过在单轮车、四旋翼无人机和Franka机械臂模型上的仿真实验验证，该框架展现了卓越的性能，速度提升最高可达139.6倍。

Conclusion: cuNRTO框架成功将高性能计算（GPU/CUDA）应用于鲁棒轨迹优化，有效解决了SOCP计算瓶颈，为自主系统在不确定的复杂环境中实现高效、实时的鲁棒决策提供了有力工具。

Abstract: Robust trajectory optimization enables autonomous systems to operate safely under uncertainty by computing control policies that satisfy the constraints for all bounded disturbances. However, these problems often lead to large Second Order Conic Programming (SOCP) constraints, which are computationally expensive. In this work, we propose the CUDA Nonlinear Robust Trajectory Optimization (cuNRTO) framework by introducing two dynamic optimization architectures that have direct application to robust decision-making and are implemented on CUDA. The first architecture, NRTO-DR, leverages the Douglas-Rachford (DR) splitting method to solve the SOCP inner subproblems of NRTO, thereby significantly reducing the computational burden through parallel SOCP projections and sparse direct solves. The second architecture, NRTO-FullADMM, is a novel variant that further exploits the problem structure to improve scalability using the Alternating Direction Method of Multipliers (ADMM). Finally, we provide GPU implementation of the proposed methodologies using custom CUDA kernels for SOC projection steps and cuBLAS GEMM chains for feedback gain updates. We validate the performance of cuNRTO through simulated experiments on unicycle, quadcopter, and Franka manipulator models, demonstrating speedup up to 139.6$\times$.

</details>


### [10] [PathSpace: Rapid continuous map approximation for efficient SLAM using B-Splines in constrained environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02538)
*Aduen Benjumea,Andrew Bradley,Alexander Rast,Matthias Rolf*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: PathSpace是一种基于B样条的语义SLAM新框架，利用连续概率密度函数在自主赛车场景中实现紧凑环境表示与高效推理。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语义SLAM技术主要依赖稠密几何表示，限制了其利用上下文约束进行推理的能力；需要一种更紧凑、能保持概率推理能力的表示方法以提升决策效率。

Method: 提出PathSpace框架，采用连续B样条（B-splines）对稀疏离散环境进行插值拟合，同时维护并推理所需的连续概率密度函数（PDF），以支持概率推理和上下文约束应用。

Abstract: Simultaneous Localization and Mapping (SLAM) plays a crucial role in enabling autonomous vehicles to navigate previously unknown environments.
  Semantic SLAM mostly extends visual SLAM, leveraging the higher density information available to reason about the environment in a more human-like manner. This allows for better decision making by exploiting prior structural knowledge of the environment, usually in the form of labels. Current semantic SLAM techniques still mostly rely on a dense geometric representation of the environment, limiting their ability to apply constraints based on context. We propose PathSpace, a novel semantic SLAM framework that uses continuous B-splines to represent the environment in a compact manner, while also maintaining and reasoning through the continuous probability density functions required for probabilistic reasoning. This system applies the multiple strengths of B-splines in the context of SLAM to interpolate and fit otherwise discrete sparse environments. We test this framework in the context of autonomous racing, where we exploit pre-specified track characteristics to produce significantly reduced representations at comparable levels of accuracy to traditional landmark based methods and demonstrate its potential in limiting the resources used by a system with minimal accuracy loss.

Unlike prior methods that restrict planning to predefined skills, Uni-Skill requests for new skill implementations when existing ones are insufficient, ensuring adaptable planning with self-augmented skill library. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散模型擅长短视界机器人规划，但受计算限制和训练数据不足影响，难以扩展到长视界任务。现有的组合方法通过分别去噪各片段并平均重叠区域来拼接，但由于噪声空间中的因子化假设失效，导致全局计划不一致和不稳定。

Method: 将长视界规划建模为重叠视频块的链式结构因子图上的推理过程，利用预训练的短视界视频扩散模型作为局部先验。在推理阶段，提出一种结合同步和异步消息传递的新机制，在Tweedie估计（清洁数据估计）上强制执行边界一致性，从而生成全局一致的引导，且无需额外训练。

Result: 该无训练框架在性能上显著优于现有基线方法，能够有效泛化到训练数据中未出现的起始-目标组合，实现了稳定的长视界规划。

Conclusion: 在清洁数据空间（Tweedie估计）上强制边界一致性是实现稳定组合生成的关键，该方法成功克服了噪声空间中因子化假设失效的问题，为长视界机器人规划提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Diffusion models excel at short-horizon robot planning, yet scaling them to long-horizon tasks remains challenging due to computational constraints and limited training data. Existing compositional approaches stitch together short segments by separately denoising each component and averaging overlapping regions. However, this suffers from instability as the factorization assumption breaks down in noisy data space, leading to inconsistent global plans. We propose that the key to stable compositional generation lies in enforcing boundary agreement on the estimated clean data (Tweedie estimates) rather than on noisy intermediate states. Our method formulates long-horizon planning as inference over a chain-structured factor graph of overlapping video chunks, where pretrained short-horizon video diffusion models provide local priors. At inference time, we enforce boundary agreement through a novel combination of synchronous and asynchronous message passing that operates on Tweedie estimates, producing globally consistent guidance without requiring additional training. Our training-free framework demonstrates significant improvements over existing baselines, effectively generalizing to unseen start-goal combinations that were not present in the original training data. Motivation: 自主无人机竞速（ADR）需要计算高效且能抵抗极端速度和机动下感知退化的状态估计。传统松散耦合的PnP校正方法存在刚性依赖四个可见特征点、中间步骤信息丢失以及在无GNSS/动捕系统环境下难以客观评估等局限。

Method: 1. ADR-VINS：采用误差状态卡尔曼滤波（ESKF），将门框角点的直接像素重投影误差作为创新项，绕过中间PnP求解器，仅需两个可见角点即可更新状态，并使用鲁棒重加权替代RANSAC处理异常值以提升效率。2. ADR-FGO：构建离线因子图优化框架，用于在无仪器环境中生成高保真参考轨迹以进行赛后评估。

Result: 在TII-RATM数据集上验证，ADR-VINS平均均方根平移误差为0.134米，ADR-FGO生成的平滑参考轨迹误差为0.060米。系统在A2RL无人机锦标赛第二季成功部署，在20.9 m/s的高速及高敏捷飞行中，面对噪声检测仍能保持稳定的状态估计。

Conclusion: 所提出的ADR-VINS和ADR-FGO框架有效解决了无GNSS环境下自主无人机竞速的状态估计难题，实现了计算高效、鲁棒性强的高精度导航，并通过离线优化框架弥补了实时评估的困难，为未仪器化竞速环境提供了可靠的性能分析手段。

Abstract: Autonomous drone racing (ADR) demands state estimation that is simultaneously computationally efficient and resilient to the perceptual degradation experienced during extreme velocity and maneuvers. Traditional frameworks typically rely on conventional visual-inertial pipelines with loosely-coupled gate-based Perspective-n-Points (PnP) corrections that suffer from a rigid requirement for four visible features and information loss in intermediate steps. Furthermore, the absence of GNSS and Motion Capture systems in uninstrumented, competitive racing environments makes the objective evaluation of such systems remarkably difficult. To address these limitations, we propose ADR-VINS, a robust, monocular visual-inertial state estimation framework based on an Error-State Kalman Filter (ESKF) tailored for autonomous drone racing. Our approach integrates direct pixel reprojection errors from gate corners features as innovation terms within the filter. By bypassing intermediate PnP solvers, ADR-VINS maintains valid state updates with as few as two visible corners and utilizes robust reweighting instead of RANSAC-based schemes to handle outliers, enhancing computational efficiency. Furthermore, we introduce ADR-FGO, an offline Factor-Graph Optimization framework to generate high-fidelity reference trajectories that facilitate post-flight performance evaluation and analysis on uninstrumented, GNSS-denied environments. The proposed system is validated using TII-RATM dataset, where ADR-VINS achieves an average RMS translation error of 0.134 m, while ADR-FGO yields 0.060 m as a smoothing-based reference. Finally, ADR-VINS was successfully deployed in the A2RL Drone Championship Season 2, maintaining stable and robust estimation despite noisy detections during high-agility flight at top speeds of 20.9 m/s. We further utilize ADR-FGO for post-flight evaluation in uninstrumented racing environments.

</details>

*Sayang Mu,Xiangyu Wu,Bo An*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有学习到的通信方法在处理空间邻近的机器人时未区分其空间距离，导致在高密度拥堵区域协调效率低下，注意力被稀释。

Result: 在40x40网格上从8个训练机器人零样本泛化至128个测试机器人，在30%障碍物密度下成功率达到约75%，优于最佳基线超过25个百分点；消融实验证实距离关系编码是提升高密度环境成功率的关键因素。

Conclusion: 通过显式嵌入空间距离信息，RMHA使机器人能动态优先处理空间相关邻居的消息，显著提升了多机器人系统在复杂和高密度环境下的协作决策与路径规划性能。

Abstract: Efficient communication is critical for decentralized Multi-Robot Path Planning (MRPP), yet existing learned communication methods treat all neighboring robots equally regardless of their spatial proximity, leading to diluted attention in congested regions where coordination matters most. We propose Relation enhanced Multi Head Attention (RMHA), a communication mechanism that explicitly embeds pairwise Manhattan distances into the attention weight computation, enabling each robot to dynamically prioritize messages from spatially relevant neighbors. Combined with a distance-constrained attention mask and GRU gated message fusion, RMHA integrates seamlessly with MAPPO for stable end-to-end training. In zero-shot generalization from 8 training robots to 128 test robots on 40x40 grids, RMHA achieves approximately 75 percent success rate at 30 percent obstacle density outperforming the best baseline by over 25 percentage points. Ablation studies confirm that distance-relation encoding is the key contributor to success rate improvement in high-density environments. Index Terms-Multi-robot path planning, graph attention mechanism, multi-head attention, communication optimization, cooperative decision-making

### [21] [CoFL: Continuous Flow Fields for Language-Conditioned Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02854)
*Haokun Liu,Zhaoqi Ma,Yicheng Chen,Masaki Kitagawa,Wentao Zhang,Jinjie Li,Moju Zhao*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: CoFL 是一种端到端导航策略，直接将鸟瞰图（BEV）观测和语言指令映射为连续流场，通过数值积分生成平滑轨迹，解决了传统模块化组件脆弱或动作序列生成成本高的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于语言的导航管道通常依赖脆弱的模块化组件或昂贵的动作序列生成方法，缺乏在未见场景下的鲁棒性和实时反应能力。

Method: 提出 CoFL 模型，直接输出瞬时速度场而非离散动作令牌；构建包含超过 50 万对 BEV 图像-指令的大规模数据集，数据源自 Matterport3D 和 ScanNet 的语义地图并经过程序化标注；采用混合分布进行训练。

Result: 在严格未见过的场景中，CoFL 显著优于基于模块化视觉 - 语言模型（VLM）的规划器和生成式策略基线；在真实世界的零样本部署实验中，保持可靠的闭环控制和高成功率。

Conclusion: CoFL 通过端到端的流场预测实现了高效、平滑且具反应性的语言条件导航，证明了其在大规模训练和真实世界复杂布局中的有效性与泛化能力。

Abstract: Language-conditioned navigation pipelines often rely on brittle modular components or costly action-sequence generation. To address these limitations, we present CoFL, an end-to-end policy that directly maps a bird's-eye view (BEV) observation and a language instruction to a continuous flow field for navigation. Instead of predicting discrete action tokens or sampling action chunks via iterative denoising, CoFL outputs instantaneous velocities that can be queried at arbitrary 2D projected locations. Trajectories are obtained by numerical integration of the predicted field, producing smooth motion that remains reactive under closed-loop execution. To enable large-scale training, we build a dataset of over 500k BEV image-instruction pairs, each procedurally annotated with a flow field and a trajectory derived from BEV semantic maps built on Matterport3D and ScanNet. By training on a mixed distribution, CoFL significantly outperforms modular Vision-Language Model (VLM)-based planners and generative policy baselines on strictly unseen scenes. Finally, we deploy CoFL zero-shot in real-world experiments with overhead BEV observations across multiple layouts, maintaining reliable closed-loop control and a high success rate.

### [25] [DreamFlow: Local Navigation Beyond Observation via Conditional Flow Matching in the Latent Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02976)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出 DreamFlow 框架，核心是一个基于条件流匹配（CFM）的预测模块。该模块学习局部高度图潜在表示与更广泛空间表示之间的概率映射，并以导航上下文为条件，使策略能够预测未观测到的环境特征。

Abstract: Local navigation in cluttered environments often suffers from dense obstacles and frequent local minima. Conventional local planners rely on heuristics and are prone to failure, while deep reinforcement learning(DRL)based approaches provide adaptability but are constrained by limited onboard sensing. These limitations lead to navigation failures because the robot cannot perceive structures outside its field of view. In this paper, we propose DreamFlow, a DRL-based local navigation framework that extends the robot's perceptual horizon through conditional flow matching(CFM). The proposed CFM based prediction module learns probabilistic mapping between local height map latent representation and broader spatial representation conditioned on navigation context. This enables the navigation policy to predict unobserved environmental features and proactively avoid potential local minima. Experimental results demonstrate that DreamFlow outperforms existing methods in terms of latent prediction accuracy and navigation performance in simulation. The proposed method was further validated in cluttered real world environments with a quadrupedal robot. The project page is available at https://dreamflow-icra.github.io.

### [26] [CASSR: Continuous A-Star Search through Reachability for real time footstep planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02989)
*Jiayi Wang,Steve Tonneau*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: CASSR是一种结合A*搜索与连续凸约束递归传播的新框架，配合基于EPA算法的启发式函数，能在125毫秒内高效规划高达30步的足步序列，显著优于传统离散化A*和商业MIP求解器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的A*方法需要离散化可达性约束，而混合整数规划（MIP）虽支持连续公式但计算复杂度高、难以扩展，特别是在包含旋转的情况下迅速变得不可行。因此，需要一种既能保持连续性又能高效处理大规模组合搜索的足步规划方法。

Method: 提出CASSR框架，在A*搜索中递归传播机器人运动学约束的凸连续形式；同时引入一种基于EPA（Expanding Polytope Algorithm）的新型代价估计启发式函数，以提升搜索效率。

Result: 实验表明，CASSR在双足行走任务中规划最多30步足步序列的时间不超过125毫秒；相比传统离散化A*方法性能提升达100倍，并优于商业MIP求解器，实现了快速、可靠且实时的足步规划。

Conclusion: CASSR成功解决了足步规划中的组合搜索难题，通过融合连续约束与高效启发式策略，为双足机器人提供了实时、可扩展且鲁棒的足部接触序列规划方案。

Abstract: Footstep planning involves a challenging combinatorial search. Traditional A* approaches require discretising reachability constraints, while Mixed-Integer Programming (MIP) supports continuous formulations but quickly becomes intractable, especially when rotations are included. We present CASSR, a novel framework that recursively propagates convex, continuous formulations of a robot's kinematic constraints within an A* search. Combined with a new cost-to-go heuristic based on the EPA algorithm, CASSR efficiently plans contact sequences of up to 30 footsteps in under 125 ms. Experiments on biped locomotion tasks demonstrate that CASSR outperforms traditional discretised A* by up to a factor of 100, while also surpassing a commercial MIP solver. These results show that CASSR enables fast, reliable, and real-time footstep planning for biped robots.

### [27] [Architectural HRI: Towards a Robotic Paradigm Shift in Human-Building Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03052)

TL;DR: 本文提出建筑与人交互（HBI）正经历范式转变，从被动服务转向通过机器人技术实现建筑空间的物理变形与重构。作者呼吁跨学科研究，以解决该领域在时空与社会复杂性上的挑战，并促进人机交互（HRI）知识向非常规建筑形态的转移。

Motivation: 随着传感、通信、控制及机器人技术的进步，建筑层能够通过物理执行器协同适应居住者需求与可持续性目标。同时，现有机器人家具和形状变化空间的研究表明，将建筑元素机器人化已成为可能。然而，当前研究面临多学科知识碎片化的问题，且缺乏对建筑环境中复杂时空与社会因素的整合理解。

Conclusion: 为了实现建筑空间机器人化的潜力，必须开展跨学科研究，打破学科壁垒，统一理论框架，以应对建筑HRI特有的复杂性，推动从自适应服务到物理空间重塑的根本性转变。

Abstract: Recent advances in sensing, communication, interfaces, control, and robotics are expanding Human-Building Interaction (HBI) beyond adaptive building services and facades toward the physical actuation of architectural space. We propose that these advances promise a paradigm shift in HBI, in which multiple building layers physically adapt in synchrony to support occupant needs and sustainability goals more holistically. Conversely, we argue that this emerging paradigm also provides an ideal case for transferring HRI knowledge to unconventional robotic morphologies, including the interpretation of the robot as multiple architectural layers or even as a building. However, this research agenda remains challenged by the temporal, spatial, and social complexity of architectural HRI, and by fragmented knowledge across HCI, environmental psychology, cognitive science, and architecture. To address this, we propose a method that leverages efficient and accessible simulators for task execution. ### [29] [Look Forward to Walk Backward: Efficient Terrain Memory for Backward Locomotion with Forward Vision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03138)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出LF2WB（Look Forward to Walk Backward）地形记忆 locomotion 框架。该方法在前向运动期间利用前向自视角深度和本体感知写入紧凑的关联记忆；在后退时检索该记忆以实现无碰撞运动。记忆骨干采用基于delta规则的增量更新机制，在活跃子空间上软性地移除并写入记忆状态。训练采用硬件高效的并行计算，部署时进行递归推理，每步推理时间为常数，状态大小固定。

Result: 仿真和真实世界实验表明，该方法在有限感知条件下显著提升了机器人在复杂地形上的后退敏捷性，实现了无碰撞的后退运动，证明了其有效性。

Conclusion: LF2WB框架成功解决了四足机器人在无后视条件下的后退难题，通过高效的地形记忆机制，使得低成本机器人也能在复杂地形上实现稳健的前后双向机动，为受限感知下的移动提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: Legged robots with egocentric forward-facing depth cameras can couple exteroception and proprioception to achieve robust forward agility on complex terrain. When these robots walk backward, the forward-only field of view provides no preview. Purely proprioceptive controllers can remain stable on moderate ground when moving backward but cannot fully exploit the robot's capabilities on complex terrain and must collide with obstacles. We present Look Forward to Walk Backward (LF2WB), an efficient terrain-memory locomotion framework that uses forward egocentric depth and proprioception to write a compact associative memory during forward motion and to retrieve it for collision-free backward locomotion without rearward vision. The memory backbone employs a delta-rule selective update that softly removes then writes the memory state along the active subspace. Training uses hardware-efficient parallel computation, and deployment runs recurrent, constant-time per-step inference with a constant-size state, making the approach suitable for onboard processors on low-cost robots. Experiments in both simulations and real-world scenarios demonstrate the effectiveness of our method, improving backward agility across complex terrains under limited sensing.

### [31] [ACE-Brain-0: Spatial Intelligence as a Shared Scaffold for Universal Embodiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03198)

Abstract: Universal embodied intelligence demands robust generalization across heterogeneous embodiments, such as autonomous driving, robotics, and unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs). However, existing embodied brain in training a unified model over diverse embodiments frequently triggers long-tail data, gradient interference, and catastrophic forgetting, making it notoriously difficult to balance universal generalization with domain-specific proficiency. In this report, we introduce ACE-Brain-0, a generalist foundation brain that unifies spatial reasoning, autonomous driving, and embodied manipulation within a single multimodal large language model~(MLLM). Our key insight is that spatial intelligence serves as a universal scaffold across diverse physical embodiments: although vehicles, robots, and UAVs differ drastically in morphology, they share a common need for modeling 3D mental space, making spatial cognition a natural, domain-agnostic foundation for cross-embodiment transfer. Building on this insight, we propose the Scaffold-Specialize-Reconcile~(SSR) paradigm, which first establishes a shared spatial foundation, then cultivates domain-specialized experts, and finally harmonizes them through data-free model merging. Furthermore, we adopt Group Relative Policy Optimization~(GRPO) to strengthen the model's comprehensive capability. Extensive experiments demonstrate that ACE-Brain-0 achieves competitive and even state-of-the-art performance across 24 spatial and embodiment-related benchmarks.

### [33] [Tether: Autonomous Functional Play with Correspondence-Driven Trajectory Warping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03278)
*William Liang,Sam Wang,Hung-Ju Wang,Osbert Bastani,Yecheng Jason Ma,Dinesh Jayaraman*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: Tether是一种自主功能玩耍方法，利用少量演示（≤10）和视觉语言模型，在真实世界中实现多任务、长时间的自主交互，自动生成高质量数据并提升策略性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器人领域需要一种可扩展的替代方案来应对劳动密集型的人类演示，但实现“玩耍”面临两大挑战：(1) 策略需对多样且可能分布外的环境状态具有鲁棒性；(2) 需要持续产生有用机器人体验的流程。

Method: 提出Tether方法，包含两个核心部分：首先设计一种新颖的开环策略，通过将源演示动作锚定到目标场景中的语义关键点，实现对少量演示的高效变形；其次，利用视觉语言模型的视觉理解能力，构建任务选择、执行、评估和改进的连续循环，驱动真实世界中的自主功能玩耍。

Result: 该方法在家庭多物体设置中首次实现了从少量演示开始的多小时真实世界自主多任务玩耍，生成了超过1000条专家级轨迹，训练出的闭环模仿策略性能可与人类收集的数据训练的策略相媲美。

Abstract: The ability to conduct and learn from interaction and experience is a central challenge in robotics, offering a scalable alternative to labor-intensive human demonstrations. However, realizing such "play" requires (1) a policy robust to diverse, potentially out-of-distribution environment states, and (2) a procedure that continuously produces useful robot experience. To address these challenges, we introduce Tether, a method for autonomous functional play involving structured, task-directed interactions. First, we design a novel open-loop policy that warps actions from a small set of source demonstrations (<=10) by anchoring them to semantic keypoint correspondences in the target scene. We show that this design is extremely data-efficient and robust even under significant spatial and semantic variations. Second, we deploy this policy for autonomous functional play in the real world via a continuous cycle of task selection, execution, evaluation, and improvement, guided by the visual understanding capabilities of vision-language models. This procedure generates diverse, high-quality datasets with minimal human intervention. In a household-like multi-object setup, our method is the first to perform many hours of autonomous multi-task play in the real world starting from only a handful of demonstrations. This produces a stream of data that consistently improves the performance of closed-loop imitation policies over time, ultimately yielding over 1000 expert-level trajectories and training policies competitive with those learned from human-collected demonstrations.

### [34] [ULTRA: Unified Multimodal Control for Autonomous Humanoid Whole-Body Loco-Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03279)

Abstract: Achieving autonomous and versatile whole-body loco-manipulation remains a central barrier to making humanoids practically useful. Yet existing approaches are fundamentally constrained: retargeted data are often scarce or low-quality; methods struggle to scale to large skill repertoires; and, most importantly, they rely on tracking predefined motion references rather than generating behavior from perception and high-level task specifications. To address these limitations, we propose ULTRA, a unified framework with two key components. First, we introduce a physics-driven neural retargeting algorithm that translates large-scale motion capture to humanoid embodiments while preserving physical plausibility for contact-rich interactions. Second, we learn a unified multimodal controller that supports both dense references and sparse task specifications, under sensing ranging from accurate motion-capture state to noisy egocentric visual inputs. We distill a universal tracking policy into this controller, compress motor skills into a compact latent space, and apply reinforcement learning finetuning to expand coverage and improve robustness under out-of-distribution scenarios. This enables coordinated whole-body behavior from sparse intent without test-time reference motions. We evaluate ULTRA in simulation and on a real Unitree G1 humanoid. Results show that ULTRA generalizes to autonomous, goal-conditioned whole-body loco-manipulation from egocentric perception, consistently outperforming tracking-only baselines with limited skills.

### [35] [How to Peel with a Knife: Aligning Fine-Grained Manipulation with Human Preference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03280)
*Toru Lin,Shuying Deng,Zhao-Heng Yin,Pieter Abbeel,Jitendra Malik*

Main category: cs.RO

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多关键的操作任务（如食品制备、手术、工艺制作）对自主机器人而言仍难以解决。这些任务不仅涉及复杂的多接触和力敏感动力学，还具有“隐性”的成功标准：任务质量是连续且主观的（例如土豆削得有多好），这使得传统的定量评估和奖励工程变得极其困难。

Method: 采用两阶段流水线方法：第一阶段，通过力感知数据收集和模仿学习，训练出具有鲁棒性的初始策略，使其能够适应物体的变化；第二阶段，利用偏好微调（preference-based finetuning）优化策略，该方法结合了一个融合定量任务指标与定性人类反馈的学习奖励模型，使策略行为与人类对任务质量的认知对齐。

Result: 仅使用50-200条削皮轨迹，该系统在黄瓜、苹果和土豆等具有挑战性的农产品上实现了超过90%的平均成功率。通过基于偏好的微调，性能提升了高达40%。此外，在单一类别上训练的策略表现出强大的零样本泛化能力，能够处理未见过的同类实例以及来自不同类别的分布外产品，同时保持90%以上的成功率。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了结合力感知模仿学习与基于人类偏好的奖励微调，能够有效解决具有隐性质量标准的复杂机器人操作任务。这种方法不仅显著提高了任务成功率，还赋予了模型极强的泛化能力，为未来处理非结构化环境下的精细操作任务提供了可行的解决方案。

Abstract: Many essential manipulation tasks - such as food preparation, surgery, and craftsmanship - remain intractable for autonomous robots. These tasks are characterized not only by contact-rich, force-sensitive dynamics, but also by their "implicit" success criteria: unlike pick-and-place, task quality in these domains is continuous and subjective (e.g. how well a potato is peeled), making quantitative evaluation and reward engineering difficult. We present a learning framework for such tasks, using peeling with a knife as a representative example. Our approach follows a two-stage pipeline: first, we learn a robust initial policy via force-aware data collection and imitation learning, enabling generalization across object variations; second, we refine the policy through preference-based finetuning using a learned reward model that combines quantitative task metrics with qualitative human feedback, aligning policy behavior with human notions of task quality. Using only 50-200 peeling trajectories, our system achieves over 90% average success rates on challenging produce including cucumbers, apples, and potatoes, with performance improving by up to 40% through preference-based finetuning. Remarkably, policies trained on a single produce category exhibit strong zero-shot generalization to unseen in-category instances and to out-of-distribution produce from different categories while maintaining over 90% success rates.

</details>

# cs.DC [[Back]](#toc)

### [36] [Why Atomicity Matters to AI/ML Infrastructure: Snapshots, Firmware Updates, and the Cost of the Forward-In-Time-Only Category Mistake](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02603)
*Paul Borrill*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 论文揭示了大规模AI训练系统依赖的两个关键假设（检查点是全局状态的原子快照、基础设施更新不会引发混合协议状态）存在深层的“仅向前时间”（FITO）结构性错误。作者通过形式化证明，在异步系统中不存在真正的原子性时间边界，并提出了基于约束语义的双向收敛协议来替代原有假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大规模AI/ML训练系统在检查点机制和固件更新策略上，往往忽略了异步环境下“时间快照”与“协议收敛”之间的本质区别，导致对系统一致性和原子性的误判，进而引发隐蔽的系统故障和优化失效。

Method: 1. 将时间快照 $\mathsf{Snap}(t)$ 与收敛属性 $\mathsf{Conv}(\mathcal{P},e)$ 的混淆形式化为类型错误。2. 在进程代数框架下模拟带崩溃恢复的异步执行，证明不存在作为原子性边界的瞬时时刻。3. 在时期格（epoch lattice）上重新表述检查点不一致性，量化原子性为测度零事件。4. 将混合时期恢复形式化为优化代数中的类型违规。5. 针对固件集群更新，强化共识硬度结果，证明原子部署所需的“共同知识”在异步不可靠通信中不可达。6. 设计受Open Atomic Ethernet启发的双向收敛协议。

Result: 证明了在异步组合且存在崩溃恢复的情况下，任何时间点都无法充当原子性边界；原子性在独立持久域数量增加时呈指数级消失；混合时期更新并非标准优化器的有效步骤；原子部署要求共同知识，这在理论上是不可行的；提出的新协议能在不依赖原子快照的前提下实现收敛属性。

Conclusion: 应摒弃将时间快照等同于协议收敛的FITO错误假设，转而采用基于约束语义的双向收敛协议，从而在不追求不可能的原子快照情况下，确保大规模训练系统的正确性和一致性。

Abstract: Large-scale AI/ML training systems depend on two assumptions that are rarely examined: (1) that checkpoints represent atomic snapshots of global training state, and (2) that infrastructure updates can be applied without inducing mixed-protocol cluster states. Both assumptions are instances of a deeper structural error: the Forward-In-Time-Only (FITO) category mistake, which confuses protocol convergence properties with temporal predicates.
  We formalize this confusion as a type error: the identification of a temporal snapshot $\mathsf{Snap}(t)$ with a convergence property $\mathsf{Conv}(\mathcal{P},e)$. We model checkpoint execution in a process-algebraic framework and prove that under asynchronous composition with crash-recovery failures, no temporal instant can serve as an atomicity boundary. We reformulate checkpoint inconsistency on an epoch lattice and show that atomicity is a measure-zero event whose complement grows exponentially with the number of independent persistence domains. We formalize mixed-epoch recovery as a type violation in the optimization algebra and show that the resulting update is not a valid step of any standard optimizer.
  For firmware fleet updates, we strengthen the known consensus-hardness result: atomic deployment requires not merely agreement but common knowledge of the epoch transition, which is strictly unattainable in asynchronous systems with unreliable communication.
  We conclude by sketching a bilateral convergence protocol, inspired by Open Atomic Ethernet, that achieves $\mathsf{Conv}(\mathcal{P},e)$ without requiring $\mathsf{Snap}(t)$ -- replacing the FITO assumption with constraint semantics.

</details>


### [37] [Undecided State Dynamics with Many Opinions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02636)
*Colin Cooper,Frederik Mallmann-Trenn,Tomasz Radzik,Nobutaka Shimizu,Takeharu Shiraga*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文在任意初始配置和任意$2\le k\le n$的 opinon 数量下，首次为Undecided-State Dynamics (USD) 过程提供了严格的共识时间界限，分别针对gossip模型和population protocol模型给出了新的上界与下界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前的工作仅在特定限制条件下（如特定的初始配置）和有限的$k$值范围内（$k = O(\sqrt{n}/(\log n)^2)$ 或 $k = O((n/\log n)^{1/3})$）建立了USD过程的紧确共识时间界限。研究旨在突破这些限制，获得适用于更广泛场景（任意初始状态和任意$k$值）的理论保证。

Method: 研究者在gossip模型和population protocol模型两个框架下，分析了Undecided-State Dynamics过程的演化行为。通过理论推导，证明了在两种模型中，对于任意初始配置和任意数量的意见$k$，该过程达到共识的时间复杂度上界。同时，构造了特定的初始配置以证明相应的下界。

Result: 1. Gossip模型：USD在$\widetilde O(\min\{k,\sqrt n\})$个同步轮次内达成共识，概率为$1-p_{\bot}-n^{-c}$（其中$p_{\bot}$为首轮坍缩至全未决状态的概率）。
2. Population Protocol模型：USD在$\widetilde O(\min\{kn,n^{3/2}\})$次异步交互内以高概率达成共识。
3. 证明了上述上界在多项对数因子意义下是紧确的（即存在匹配的下界），表明结果是本质最优的。

Conclusion: 本文填补了Undecided-State Dynamics理论分析的空白，证明了该共识过程在更广泛的参数空间和初始条件下依然高效运行，其性能界限在理论上是最优的。这为分布式系统中的共识算法设计提供了更强的理论支撑。

Abstract: We study the Undecided-State Dynamics (USD), a fundamental consensus process in which each vertex holds one of $k$ decided opinions or the undecided state. We consider both the gossip model and the population protocol model. Prior work established tight bounds on the consensus time of this process only for the regime $k = O(\sqrt{n}/(\log n)^2)$ (for the population protocol model) and $k = O((n/\log n)^{1/3})$ (for the gossip model), often under restrictive assumptions on the initial configuration.
  In this paper, we obtain the first consensus-time guarantees for USD that hold for \emph{arbitrary} $2\le k\le n$ and for \emph{arbitrary} initial configurations in both the gossip model and the population protocol model. In the gossip model, USD reaches consensus within $\widetilde O(\min\{k,\sqrt n\})$ synchronous rounds with probability $1-p_{\bot}-n^{-c}$, where $p_{\bot}$ is the gossip-specific probability of collapsing to the all-undecided state in the first round. In the population protocol model, USD reaches consensus within $\widetilde O(\min\{kn,n^{3/2}\})$ asynchronous interactions with high probability. We also present lower bounds that match the upper bounds up to polylogarithmic factors for a specific initial configuration and show that our upper bounds are essentially optimal.

</details>

### [39] [Dynamic Contract Analysis for Parallel Programming Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03023)
*Yussur Mustafa Oraji,Alexander Hück,Christian Bischof*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 提出CoVer-Dynamic，一个结合静态与动态分析的验证框架，复用CoVer的契约语言，在MPI和OpenSHMEM基准测试中消除了误报并超越了现有工具MUST的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 并行编程依赖低层API（如MPI），需手动管理同步和资源；现有正确性检查工具多针对单一模型，且纯静态分析无法处理运行时行为（如指针别名、间接控制流）。

Method: 基于CoVer的契约语言构建动态分析扩展CoVer-Dynamic，形成统一的静-动态验证框架，在运行时强制执行相同的契约规则。

Result: 在标准MPI和OpenSHMEM基准上提升了分类准确性并消除误报，能检测静态分析遗漏的错误；相比最先进工具MUST平均快2倍。

Conclusion: 统一静-动态框架显著优于现有技术，但当前契约语言的表达能力仍有局限，未来需支持更多错误类别。

Abstract: Parallel programming in high-performance computing depends on low-level APIs such as MPI, requiring users to manage synchronization and resources manually. Several correctness checking tools exist to help bug-free code development, though most target a single programming model, limiting their applicability. Our previous work, the static analysis tool CoVer, leverages a contract-based approach enabling users to specify custom error-checking rules and support emerging or unconventional programming models without requiring extensive new tooling. However, static analysis cannot fully reason about runtime-dependent behavior such as pointer aliasing or indirect control flow. To address this, we present CoVer-Dynamic, a dynamic analysis extension that reuses CoVer's contract language to provide a unified static-dynamic verification framework. By enforcing the same contracts at runtime, CoVer-Dynamic improves classification accuracy and eliminates false positives on standardized MPI and OpenSHMEM benchmarks, while detecting errors beyond static analysis only. Our evaluation shows that CoVer-Dynamic consistently outperforms the state-of-the-art correctness checker MUST, averaging a 2x speedup. Finally, our results show limitations in the expressiveness of the contract language, motivating future work to support more error classes.

</details>


### [40] [Serverless Abstractions for Short-Running, Lightweight Streams](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03089)
*Natalie Carl,Niklas Kowallik,Constantin Stahl,Trever Schirmer,Tobias Pfandzelter,David Bermbach*

Main category: cs.DC

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Serverless计算和流处理范式均假设工作负载具有较长运行时间或可预测性，导致它们在处理短运行、轻量级且不可预测但需状态管理的流式数据时效率低下。

Method: 设计一种基于迭代器接口的流函数模型，使其在保留Serverless平台弹性伸缩和零缩容能力的同时，支持事件间逻辑处理；以短流为基本执行单元，统一管理状态与资源调度。

Result: 在视频处理用例中，流函数的处理开销较成熟流处理引擎降低约99%，同时提供与Serverless函数相当的性能表现。

Conclusion: 流函数为传统模型未能有效服务的短运行、状态化流工作负载提供了一种高效、可扩展的新抽象，填补了Serverless与流处理之间的空白。

Abstract: Serverless computing and stream processing represent two dominant paradigms for event-driven data processing, yet both make assumptions that render them inefficient for short-running, lightweight, and unpredictable streams that require stateful processing. We propose stream functions as a novel extension of the Function-as-a-Serivce model that treat short streams as the unit of execution, state, and scaling. Stream functions process streams via an iterator-based interface, enabling seamless inter-event logic while retaining the elasticity and scale-to-zero capabilities offered by serverless platforms. Our evaluation shows that stream functions reduce the processing overhead by ~99 % compared to a mature stream process- ing engine in a video-processing use case. By providing comparable performance to serverless functions with stream semantics, stream functions provide an effective and efficient abstractions for a class of workloads underserved by existing models.

### [41] [Federated Inference: Toward Privacy-Preserving Collaborative and Incentivized Model Serving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02214)
*Jungwon Seo,Ferhat Ozgur Catak,Chunming Rong,Jaeyeon Jang*

Main category: cs.AI

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究虽涉及安全分布式推理，但缺乏对联邦推理的统一抽象和系统级理解；亟需明确其作为独立范式的定义、可行性条件及设计权衡。

Method: 将FI形式化为受保护的协同计算，分析其核心设计维度，并在隐私约束、非独立同分布（Non-IID）数据和有限可观测性共同作用下考察结构性权衡；通过具体实例化与实证分析，识别隐私保护、集成协作及激励对齐中的摩擦点。

Result: 联邦推理展现出无法从训练时联邦学习或经典集成方法直接继承的系统级行为；研究揭示了隐私-性能权衡、数据异构性及激励问题带来的实际挑战。

Conclusion: 本文提供了联邦推理的统一视角，明确了实现实用、可扩展且隐私保护的协同推理系统所必须解决的关键开放性问题。

Abstract: Federated Inference (FI) studies how independently trained and privately owned models can collaborate at inference time without sharing data or model parameters. While recent work has explored secure and distributed inference from disparate perspectives, a unified abstraction and system-level understanding of FI remain lacking. This paper positions FI as a distinct collaborative paradigm, complementary to federated learning, and identifies two fundamental requirements that govern its feasibility: inference-time privacy preservation and meaningful performance gains through collaboration. We formalize FI as a protected collaborative computation, analyze its core design dimensions, and examine the structural trade-offs that arise when privacy constraints, non-IID data, and limited observability are jointly imposed at inference time. Through a concrete instantiation and empirical analysis, we highlight recurring friction points in privacy-preserving inference, ensemble-based collaboration, and incentive alignment. Our findings suggest that FI exhibits system-level behaviors that cannot be directly inherited from training-time federation or classical ensemble methods. Overall, this work provides a unifying perspective on FI and outlines open challenges that must be addressed to enable practical, scalable, and privacy-preserving collaborative inference systems.

### [42] [Engineering Reasoning and Instruction (ERI) Benchmark: A Large Taxonomy-driven Dataset for Foundation Models and Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02239)
*MZ Naser,Ahmad Bani Awwad,Zoie McCreery,Radwa Eissa,Ahmad Naser,Gianluca Cusatis,Andrew Metcalf,Kapil Madathil,Jamal Abdalla,Venkatesh Kodur,Mohammad Reza Saeb*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ERI是一个面向工程领域的指令数据集基准，涵盖9个工程学科、55个子领域及7种意图类型和3个难度等级，共57,750条记录。研究评估了7个大模型，发现存在显著的三级性能结构，并提出了收敛验证协议将幻觉风险控制在1.7%以内。

Method: 构建了包含9个工程领域、55个子领域、7种意图类型（定义、解释、计算等）和3个难度层级（本科、研究生、专业）的taxonomy-driven指令数据集；通过7个LLM进行实证评估；提出基于跨提供商独立性、多法官平均和前沿模型一致性分析的收敛验证协议来量化幻觉风险。

Result: 在五点量表上，前沿模型（GPT-5, Claude Sonnet 4, DeepSeek V3.1）平均分超过4.30；中低端及小模型在研究生级问题上表现出更高的失败率和更陡峭的性能下降；成功将幻觉风险限制在1.7%以内。

Conclusion: ERI基准为工程领域的指令微调、路由、检索增强评估及智能体工具使用工作流提供了可复现的比较框架和回归测试工具，有效支持了工程大模型的研发与评估。

Abstract: The Engineering Reasoning and Instruction (ERI) benchmark is a taxonomy-driven instruction dataset designed to train and evaluate engineering-capable large language models (LLMs) and agents. This dataset spans nine engineering fields (namely: civil, mechanical, electrical, chemical, environmental, aerospace, materials, fire, and industrial engineering) and 55 subdomains, and is crossed with seven intent types (i.e., definition, explanation, calculation, comparison, design/synthesis, troubleshooting, and code-related) and three difficulty tiers (undergraduate, graduate, and professional), yielding 57,750 records with field/subdomain/type/difficulty metadata and solution formatting. We examined ERI via seven LLMs and report a statistically significant three-tier performance structure, with frontier models (GPT-5, Claude Sonnet 4, DeepSeek V3.1) achieving mean scores above 4.30 on a five-point scale, while mid-tier and smaller models exhibited progressively higher failure rates and steeper performance degradation on graduate-level questions. To address circularity concerns inherent in LLM benchmarks, we developed a convergent validation protocol that leverages cross-provider independence, multi-judge averaging, and frontier-model agreement analysis to empirically bound hallucination risk to 1.7%. ERI is released with taxonomy specifications, validation scripts, and an evaluation harness to enable reproducible comparisons and regression testing for instruction tuning, routing, retrieval-augmented evaluation, and agentic tool-use workflows in engineering settings.

</details>


### [43] [Estimating Visual Attribute Effects in Advertising from Observational Data: A Deepfake-Informed Double Machine Learning Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02359)
*Yizhi Liu,Balaji Padmanabhan,Siva Viswanathan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出DICE-DML框架，利用生成式AI（Deepfake）分离图像中的处理变量与混淆变量，解决视觉数据因果推断的偏差问题。在模拟中误差降低73-97%，应用于Instagram数据发现肤色对互动量的负面影响被传统方法严重高估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数字广告依赖视觉内容，但缺乏严谨方法来理解特定视觉属性（如模特肤色）如何因果性地影响消费者参与度。标准方法（如双重机器学习DML）因视觉编码器将处理信息与混淆变量纠缠在一起，导致估计严重偏差。

Method: 开发DICE-DML框架，结合三种机制：(1) 使用Deepfake生成的成对图像隔离处理变量的变化；(2) 在成对差异向量上进行DICE-Diff对抗学习，抵消背景信号以揭示纯处理特征；(3) 正交投影几何移除处理轴分量。

Result: 在已知真实值的模拟中，相比标准DML，DICE-DML将均方根误差降低73-97%（null effect点处降低97.5%），表现出稳健的第一类错误控制。应用于232,089条Instagram帖子时，标准DML产生无效诊断结果（负R²），而DICE-DML实现有效混淆控制（R²=0.63），估算出较暗肤色的负面影响为减少约522个赞（p=0.062），显著小于传统方法的有偏估计。

Conclusion: 该框架为当处理变量与混淆变量共存于图像内时的视觉数据因果推断提供了原则性的解决方案，解决了现有方法无法有效分离视觉特征的难题。

Abstract: Digital advertising increasingly relies on visual content, yet marketers lack rigorous methods for understanding how specific visual attributes causally affect consumer engagement. This paper addresses a fundamental methodological challenge: estimating causal effects when the treatment, such as a model's skin tone, is an attribute embedded within the image itself. Standard approaches like Double Machine Learning (DML) fail in this setting because vision encoders entangle treatment information with confounding variables, producing severely biased estimates. We develop DICE-DML (Deepfake-Informed Control Encoder for Double Machine Learning), a framework that leverages generative AI to disentangle treatment from confounders. The approach combines three mechanisms: (1) deepfake-generated image pairs that isolate treatment variation; (2) DICE-Diff adversarial learning on paired difference vectors, where background signals cancel to reveal pure treatment fingerprints; and (3) orthogonal projection that geometrically removes treatment-axis components. In simulations with known ground truth, DICE-DML reduces root mean squared error by 73-97% compared to standard DML, with the strongest improvement (97.5%) at the null effect point, demonstrating robust Type I error control. Applying DICE-DML to 232,089 Instagram influencer posts, we estimate the causal effect of skin tone on engagement. Standard DML produces diagnostically invalid results (negative outcome R^2), while DICE-DML achieves valid confounding control (R^2 = 0.63) and estimates a marginally significant negative effect of darker skin tone (-522 likes; p = 0.062), substantially smaller than the biased standard estimate. Our framework provides a principled approach for causal inference with visual data when treatments and confounders coexist within images.

</details>


### [44] [EvoSkill: Automated Skill Discovery for Multi-Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02766)
*Salaheddin Alzubi,Noah Provenzano,Jaydon Bingham,Weiyuan Chen,Tu Vu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: EvoSkill是一个自进化框架，通过迭代失败分析自动发现和优化智能体技能（Agent Skills），在OfficeQA和SealQA两个基准测试中分别提升了7.3%和12.1%的准确率，并展现出跨任务的零样本迁移能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的编码智能体缺乏特定领域的专业知识，而当前基于“智能体技能”的解决方案多依赖人工制作，且现有的进化方法仅优化与特定模型和任务紧密耦合的低层工件（如提示词和代码），缺乏通用性和可复用性。

Method: 提出EvoSkill框架，通过分析执行失败来自动生成或修改技能，并将结果物化为结构化的技能文件夹；利用帕累托前沿（Pareto frontier）筛选仅在冻结底层模型的情况下能提升验证集性能的技能。

Result: 在OfficeQA基准上将精确匹配准确率从60.6%提升至67.9%（+7.3%）；在SealQA基准上从26.6%提升至38.7%（+12.1%）；此外，在SealQA上进化的技能可零样本迁移至BrowseComp任务，准确率提升5.3%。

Conclusion: 基于技能层面的优化能够产生超越训练任务的、可迁移的能力，证明了自动化发现技能比人工构建或低层优化更具优势。

Abstract: Coding agents are increasingly used as general-purpose problem solvers, but their flexibility does not by itself confer the domain expertise needed for specialized tasks. Recent work addresses this through \textit{agent skills}: reusable workflows, and code, that augment agents with domain-specific capabilities. Most skills today are hand-crafted, and existing evolutionary approaches optimize low-level artifacts (e.g. prompts \& code) that are tightly coupled to specific models and tasks. We introduce \textbf{EvoSkill}, a self-evolving framework that automatically discovers and refines agent skills through iterative failure analysis. EvoSkill analyzes execution failures, proposes new skills or edits to existing ones, and materializes them into structured, reusable skill folders. A Pareto frontier of agent programs governs selection, retaining only skills that improve held-out validation performance while the underlying model remains frozen. We evaluate EvoSkill on two benchmarks: OfficeQA, a grounded reasoning benchmark over U.S.\ Treasury data, where it improves exact-match accuracy by \textbf{7.3\%} (60.6\% $\to$ 67.9\%); and SealQA, a search-augmented QA benchmark with noisy retrieval, where it yields a \textbf{12.1\%} gain (26.6\% $\to$ 38.7\%). We also investigate the zero-shot transfer capabilties of skills evolved on one task to the other; in particular: skills evolved from SealQA transfers zero-shot to BrowseComp, improving accuracy by \textbf{5.3\%} without modification demonstrating that skill-level optimization produces transferable capabilities beyond the training task.

### [45] [Can machines be uncertain?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02365)
*Luis Rosa*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文从功能主义和行为视角探讨AI系统如何实现不确定性状态，区分了认识论不确定性与主观不确定性，并提出部分不确定性是“疑问态度”而非命题内容。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在厘清AI系统中“不确定性”的实现机制，特别是如何区分数据层面的不确定性与系统自身表现出的不确定态度，并探索不同架构（符号、连接主义、混合）对这一状态的承载能力。

Method: 采用功能主义和行为主义分析框架，对比符号、连接主义及混合架构处理不确定性的方式；通过概念分析区分认识论不确定性与主观不确定性，并进一步将主观不确定性划分为分布式与离散化实现；引入“疑问态度”概念重构不确定性的语义内容。

Conclusion: 理解AI的不确定性需超越单纯的数据概率模型，将其视为一种具有特定意向性结构的认知状态；该框架为设计具备真正不确定性感知能力的智能系统提供了理论依据。

Abstract: The paper investigates whether and how AI systems can realize states of uncertainty. The paper distinguishes between epistemic uncertainty, or uncertainty inherent in the data or information, and subjective uncertainty, or the system's own attitude of being uncertainty. It further distinguishes between distributed and discrete realizations of subjective uncertainty. A key contribution is the idea that some states of uncertainty are interrogative attitudes whose content is a question rather than a proposition.

Abstract: Real-world multimodal knowledge graphs (MKGs) are inherently heterogeneous, modeling entities that are associated with diverse modalities. ### [47] [Diagnosing Retrieval vs. Utilization Bottlenecks in LLM Agent Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02473)
*Boqin Yuan,Yue Su,Kun Yao*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 在当前检索实践下，提升检索质量比增加写入时的复杂性更能显著提升智能体性能；现有记忆管道可能因过度处理而丢弃了下游检索机制无法补偿的有效上下文。

Abstract: Memory-augmented LLM agents store and retrieve information from prior interactions, yet the relative importance of how memories are written versus how they are retrieved remains unclear. We introduce a diagnostic framework that analyzes how performance differences manifest across write strategies, retrieval methods, and memory utilization behavior, and apply it to a 3x3 study crossing three write strategies (raw chunks, Mem0-style fact extraction, MemGPT-style summarization) with three retrieval methods (cosine, BM25, hybrid reranking). On LoCoMo, retrieval method is the dominant factor: average accuracy spans 20 points across retrieval methods (57.1% to 77.2%) but only 3-8 points across write strategies. Raw chunked storage, which requires zero LLM calls, matches or outperforms expensive lossy alternatives, suggesting that current memory pipelines may discard useful context that downstream retrieval mechanisms fail to compensate for. Failure analysis shows that performance breakdowns most often manifest at the retrieval stage rather than at utilization. We argue that, under current retrieval practices, improving retrieval quality yields larger gains than increasing write-time sophistication. Code is publicly available at https://github.com/boqiny/memory-probe.

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) exhibit a unified "general factor" of capability across 10 benchmarks, a finding confirmed by our factor analysis of 156 models, yet they still struggle with simple, trivial tasks for humans. This is because current benchmarks focus on task completion, failing to probe the foundational cognitive abilities that highlight these behaviors. We address this by introducing the NeuroCognition benchmark, grounded in three adapted neuropsychological tests: Raven's Progressive Matrices (abstract relational reasoning), Spatial Working Memory (maintenance and systematic search), and the Wisconsin Card Sorting Test (cognitive flexibility). Our evaluation reveals that while models perform strongly on text, their performance degrades for images and with increased complexity. Furthermore, we observe that complex reasoning is not universally beneficial, whereas simple, human-like strategies yield partial gains. We also find that NeuroCognition correlates positively with standard general-capability benchmarks, while still measuring distinct cognitive abilities beyond them. Overall, NeuroCognition emphasizes where current LLMs align with human-like intelligence and where they lack core adaptive cognition, showing the potential to serve as a verifiable, scalable source for improving LLMs.

### [49] [SUN: Shared Use of Next-token Prediction for Efficient Multi-LLM Disaggregated Serving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02599)
*Sunghyeon Woo,Ahreum Seo,Jaegwang Lee,Jaeeun Kil,Hanbae Seo,Joonghoon Kim,Baeseong Park,Se Jung Kwon,Dongsoo Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SUN通过解耦Transformer的预填充和解码模块，实现了多LLM服务中解码执行跨模型共享，显著提升了GPU利用率并降低了成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决多模型大语言模型（LLM）服务中因模型特定资源分区导致的解码执行效率低下问题，特别是由于无法进行跨模型批处理而造成的显存受限解码过程中严重的GPU资源浪费，尤其是在负载分布不均的情况下。

Method: 提出名为“共享下一个词预测”（SUN）的方法，将Decoder-only Transformer分解为预填充模块和解码模块；仅微调任务特定的预填充模块，使解码模块保持冻结并可被多个模型共享；设计了一种与模型无关的解码路由策略，以在共享工作节点间平衡解码请求，最大化系统利用率。此外，提出了量化版本QSUN以支持低比特解码。

Result: 在多样任务和模型家族中，SUN保持了与全量微调相当的高精度，同时使用更少的解码工作节点维持了系统吞吐量。相比传统解离方案，SUN将每GPU吞吐量最高提升了2.0倍，且输出令牌时间（TPOT）增加不超过5%。结合量化技术后，QSUN在保持共享解码优势的同时，实现了45%的速度提升且精度相当。

Conclusion: SUN通过架构解耦和参数共享机制，有效解决了多模型LLM服务中的资源碎片化问题，不仅大幅提升了系统吞吐效率和硬件利用率，还天然支持低比特量化加速，为构建高效、可扩展的多模型LLM服务平台提供了新范式。

Abstract: In multi-model LLM serving, decode execution remains inefficient due to model-specific resource partitioning: since cross-model batching is not possible, memory-bound decoding often suffers from severe GPU underutilization, especially under skewed workloads. We propose Shared Use of Next-token Prediction (SUN), the first approach that enables cross-model sharing of decode execution in disaggregated multi-LLM serving. SUN decomposes a decoder-only Transformer into a prefill module and a decode module, and fine-tunes only the task-specific prefill module, enabling a frozen decode module to be shared across models. This design enables a model-agnostic decode routing policy that balances decode requests across shared workers to maximize utilization. Across diverse tasks and model families, SUN achieves accuracy comparable to full fine-tuning while maintaining system throughput with fewer decode workers. In particular, SUN improves throughput per GPU by up to 2.0x over conventional disaggregation while keeping time-per-output-token (TPOT) within 5%. SUN inherently enables and facilitates low-bit decoding; with Quantized SUN (QSUN), it achieves a 45% speedup with comparable accuracy to SUN while preserving the benefits of shared decoding.

### [50] [AgentAssay: Token-Efficient Regression Testing for Non-Deterministic AI Agent Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02601)
*Varun Pratap Bhardwaj*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AgentAssay 是一个针对非确定性 AI 智能体工作流的第一个令牌高效回归测试框架，通过统计假设检验和行为指纹技术，实现了78-100%的成本降低，同时保持严格的统计保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着自主AI智能体以前所未有的规模部署，目前缺乏一种原则性的方法来验证在提示词、工具、模型或编排逻辑发生变化后，智能体是否发生了性能退化（回归）。现有的测试方法无法有效应对智能体的非确定性特征。

Method: 提出了一种包含八项核心贡献的方法论：(1) 基于假设检验的随机三值判定（通过/失败/不确定）；(2) 五维智能体覆盖率指标；(3) 特定于智能体的变异测试算子；(4) 智能体工作流的多态关系；(5) 作为统计决策过程的CI/CD部署门禁；(6) 将执行轨迹映射为紧凑向量的行为指纹技术，用于多元回归检测；(7) 根据行为方差校准试验次数的自适应预算优化；(8) 利用生产轨迹进行零成本测试的“轨迹优先”离线分析。

Result: 在5个模型（GPT-5.2, Claude Sonnet 4.6等）、3个场景和7,605次试验的实验中，行为指纹技术在二元测试完全无效（0%检测率）的情况下实现了86%的检测能力；序贯概率比检验（SPRT）减少了78%的试验次数；而完整的流水线通过轨迹优先分析实现了100%的成本节省。

Conclusion: AgentAssay 成功解决了AI智能体回归测试中的非确定性和高成本问题，通过引入统计方法和行为指纹技术，为大规模部署的智能体提供了可信赖、低成本的验证机制，证明了其在实际工程应用中的有效性。

Abstract: Autonomous AI agents are deployed at unprecedented scale, yet no principled methodology exists for
  verifying that an agent has not regressed after changes to its prompts, tools, models, or
  orchestration logic. We present AgentAssay, the first token-efficient framework for regression
  testing non-deterministic AI agent workflows, achieving 78-100% cost reduction while maintaining
  rigorous statistical guarantees. Our contributions include: (1) stochastic three-valued verdicts
  (PASS/FAIL/INCONCLUSIVE) grounded in hypothesis testing; (2) five-dimensional agent coverage metrics;
  (3) agent-specific mutation testing operators; (4) metamorphic relations for agent workflows; (5)
  CI/CD deployment gates as statistical decision procedures; (6) behavioral fingerprinting that maps
  execution traces to compact vectors, enabling multivariate regression detection; (7) adaptive budget
  optimization calibrating trial counts to behavioral variance; and (8) trace-first offline analysis
  enabling zero-cost testing on production traces. Experiments across 5 models (GPT-5.2, Claude Sonnet
  4.6, Mistral-Large-3, Llama-4-Maverick, Phi-4), 3 scenarios, and 7,605 trials demonstrate that
  behavioral fingerprinting achieves 86% detection power where binary testing has 0%, SPRT reduces
  trials by 78%, and the full pipeline achieves 100% cost savings through trace-first analysis.
  Implementation: 20,000+ lines of Python, 751 tests, 10 framework adapters.

### [51] [LLMs for High-Frequency Decision-Making: Normalized Action Reward-Guided Consistency Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02680)
*Yang Zhao,Zihao Li,Zhiyu Jiang,Dandan Ma,Ganchao Liu,Wenzhe Zhao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对大语言模型（LLM）在高频决策任务中存在的精度不足和策略对齐问题，本文提出NAR-CP方法。该方法通过归一化动作奖励和一致性损失优化，实现了独立与复合任务上的高性能表现及泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM的决策研究多集中于低频、离散且语义差异显著的具身决策场景（如家庭规划）。然而，这些方法在处理高频决策任务时表现不佳，因为此类任务中的状态空间数值信息更新频繁且波动微小，导致学习到的子任务策略与复合任务策略之间存在错位（policy misalignment）。

Method: 提出了“归一化动作奖励引导的一致性策略优化”（NAR-CP）：1) 利用环境反馈获取候选动作的稠密奖励，并通过归一化进行奖励塑形，理论上证明了动作奖励归一化不会损害最优策略；2) 利用LLM推断子观测的候选动作并生成联合策略，引入一致性损失（consistency loss）以确保全局语义策略与子语义策略之间的精确对齐。

Result: 在无人机追逐（UAV pursuit）这一典型的高频任务上进行的实验表明，该方法在独立任务和复合任务上均表现出优越的性能，并且对未见过的任务具有出色的泛化能力。

Conclusion: NAR-CP有效解决了LLM在高频决策任务中的局限性和策略错位问题，通过奖励归一化和一致性约束，显著提升了智能体在复杂动态环境下的决策质量和泛化性能。

Abstract: While Large Language Models (LLMs) form the cornerstone of sequential decision-making agent development, they have inherent limitations in high-frequency decision tasks. Existing research mainly focuses on discrete embodied decision scenarios with low-frequency and significant semantic differences in state space (e.g., household planning). These methods suffer from limited performance in high-frequency decision-making tasks, since high-precision numerical state information in such tasks undergoes frequent updates with minimal fluctuations, and exhibiting policy misalignment between the learned sub-tasks and composite tasks. To address these issues, this paper proposes Normalized Action Reward guided Consistency Policy Optimization (NAR-CP). 1) Our method first acquires predefined dense rewards from environmental feedback of candidate actions via reward functions, then completes reward shaping through normalization, and theoretically verifies action reward normalization does not impair optimal policy. 2) To reduce policy misalignment in composite tasks, we use LLMs to infer sub-observation candidate actions and generate joint policies, with consistency loss ensuring precise alignment between global semantic policies and sub-semantic policies. Experiments on UAV pursuit, a typical high-frequency task, show our method delivers superior performance on independent and composite tasks with excellent generalization to unseen tasks.

</details>


### [52] [Retrieval-Augmented Robots via Retrieve-Reason-Act](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02688)
*Izat Temiraliev,Diji Yang,Yi Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出“检索增强机器人”（RAR）范式，使机器人在零样本场景下能通过主动检索外部非结构化视觉文档来获取未知程序性知识，并通过跨模态对齐将2D图纸转化为3D物理执行计划，显著优于传统零样本推理或少样本示例检索方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器人研究在严格零样本设置下存在关键信息缺口，无法仅靠内部参数化知识或记忆解决复杂任务（如家具组装）。当前尝试“先搜索后行动”的方法多局限于检索历史运动轨迹或文本安全规则，未能解决从外部非结构化文档中获取未见过程性知识的核心需求。

Method: 提出迭代式“检索-推理-行动”（Retrieve-Reason-Act）循环：机器人从非结构化语料库中主动检索相关视觉操作手册，通过跨模态对齐将抽象的2D图表与3D物理部件进行关联，进而综合生成可执行的规划方案。

Result: 在具有挑战性的长周期组装基准测试中，基于检索到的视觉文档进行地面定位的机器人规划方法，其表现显著优于依赖零样本推理或少样本示例检索的基线方法。

Conclusion: 本研究确立了检索增强机器人（RAR）的基础，将信息检索的范畴从回答用户查询扩展至驱动具身物理动作，使机器人从被动执行者进化为主动的信息检索使用者。

Abstract: To achieve general-purpose utility, we argue that robots must evolve from passive executors into active Information Retrieval users. In strictly zero-shot settings where no prior demonstrations exist, robots face a critical information gap, such as the exact sequence required to assemble a complex furniture kit, that cannot be satisfied by internal parametric knowledge (common sense) or past internal memory. While recent robotic works attempt to use search before action, they primarily focus on retrieving past kinematic trajectories (analogous to searching internal memory) or text-based safety rules (searching for constraints). These approaches fail to address the core information need of active task construction: acquiring unseen procedural knowledge from external, unstructured documentation. In this paper, we define the paradigm as Retrieval-Augmented Robotics (RAR), empowering the robot with the information-seeking capability that bridges the gap between visual documentation and physical actuation. We formulate the task execution as an iterative Retrieve-Reason-Act loop: the robot or embodied agent actively retrieves relevant visual procedural manuals from an unstructured corpus, grounds the abstract 2D diagrams to 3D physical parts via cross-modal alignment, and synthesizes executable plans. We validate this paradigm on a challenging long-horizon assembly benchmark. Our experiments demonstrate that grounding robotic planning in retrieved visual documents significantly outperforms baselines relying on zero-shot reasoning or few-shot example retrieval. This work establishes the basis of RAR, extending the scope of Information Retrieval from answering user queries to driving embodied physical actions.

Method: 1. 从SEC文件中提取目标公司的上下文信息；2. 采用基于嵌入的匹配机制检索语义相关的新闻文章；3. 利用大语言模型（LLMs）将新闻分类为四个层级（宏观、行业、相关公司、目标公司），实现多级配对；4. 构建大规模文本配对股票价格数据集FinTexTS。

Abstract: The financial domain involves a variety of important time-series problems. Recently, time-series analysis methods that jointly leverage textual and numerical information have gained increasing attention. Accordingly, numerous efforts have been made to construct text-paired time-series datasets in the financial domain. However, financial markets are characterized by complex interdependencies, in which a company's stock price is influenced not only by company-specific events but also by events in other companies and broader macroeconomic factors. Existing approaches that pair text with financial time-series data based on simple keyword matching often fail to capture such complex relationships. To address this limitation, we propose a semantic-based and multi-level pairing framework. Specifically, we extract company-specific context for the target company from SEC filings and apply an embedding-based matching mechanism to retrieve semantically relevant news articles based on this context. Furthermore, we classify news articles into four levels (macro-level, sector-level, related company-level, and target-company level) using large language models (LLMs), enabling multi-level pairing of news articles with the target company. Applying this framework to publicly-available news datasets, we construct \textbf{FinTexTS}, a new large-scale text-paired stock price dataset. Experimental results on \textbf{FinTexTS} demonstrate the effectiveness of our semantic-based and multi-level pairing strategy in stock price forecasting. In addition to publicly-available news underlying \textbf{FinTexTS}, we show that applying our method to proprietary yet carefully curated news sources leads to higher-quality paired data and improved stock price forecasting performance.
